     <article class="main-page-content" lang="en-US">
      <h1>Web APIs</h1>
      <div>
       <p><span class="seoSummary">When writing code for the Web, there are a large number of Web APIs available. Below is a list of all the APIs and interfaces (object types) that you may be able to use while developing your Web app or site.</span></p> 
       <p>Web APIs are typically used with JavaScript, although this doesn't always have to be the case.</p>
      </div>
      <h2 id="specifications"><a href="#specifications" title="Permalink to Specifications">Specifications</a></h2>
      <div>
